The company reported net income of $244.8 million and revenues of $9.3 billion for the quarter that ended Nov. 30, 2024, compared to net income of $522.9 million and revenues of $11.4 billion in the first quarter of fiscal year 2024.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> revenues.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font market conditions negatively impacting refining margins. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font margins compared to historically high margins in the first quarter of the prior fiscal year.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font investment being the largest contributor.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;The energy industry is experiencing compressed refinery margins at the same time that U.S. agriculture is seeing a weaker farm economy with a globally competitive marketplace for grains and oilseeds,&#8221; said Jay Debertin, president and CEO of CHS Inc. &#8220;Just as we have for nearly 100 years, CHS is leveraging our efficient global supply chain, strong relationships and expertise to navigate these changing markets, while strategically investing to meet our owners&#8217; future needs.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Energy </font></div><div><font million decrease versus the prior year period and reflect&#58;</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font higher U.S. refinery capacity utilization and global production</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font offset lower income from refined fuels </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font soybean meal and oil across global markets, somewhat offset by the timing impact of market adjustments </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font As a leading global agribusiness and the largest farmer-owned cooperative in the United States, CHS serves customers in 65 countries and employs approximately 10,000 people worldwide. We provide critical crop inputs, market access and risk management services that help farmers feed the world. Our diversified agronomy, grains, foods and energy businesses recorded revenues of approximately $39 billion in fiscal year 2024. CHS is committed to reducing our impact on the planet, finding and developing new solutions in agriculture and energy, and investing in ways to build a better future for our owners, customers, employees and communities.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">This document and other CHS Inc. publicly available documents contain, and CHS officers, directors and representatives may from time to time make &#34;forward-looking statements&#34; within the meaning of the safe harbor provisions of the U.S. Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
